Silk and Tea Factories Experience Sluggish US Sales

The US raw silk market has recently been affected by the stock market decline and cheap Japanese silk sales, causing Chinese silk to become increasingly sluggish. Huangbai factories telegraphed complaining that prices were too high. B-grade 83-85 is degree 20-22. The Shanghai white factory telegraphed a price of only 523 taels, resulting in significant losses for the factory, and their attitude was negative, unwilling to sell. Yesterday, only Xinfu imported 20 bales of first-grade 13-15 degree Lu Huang factory silk at a price of 590 taels. Xiangli imported 20 bales of Globe brand second-grade Chongmian yellow coarse silk at a price of 270 taels.

Foreign Tea Market Slightly Quiet

Yesterday, the foreign tea market was slightly quiet. Various firms only traded for half a day, concluding deals for over 500 boxes of Zhenmei, Zhenmei, Xiumei, and Zhucha bulk tea. Market prices remained largely unchanged. Russian and White Head merchants did not purchase Gongxi tea. However, Road and Local merchants Zhenmei tea reportedly sent out large telegraphs through Tongfu, Xiehe, and other firms, indicating promising development in the market next week.

Sugar Market White Slices See Price Increase

Yesterday, the sugar market saw little fluctuation in the gold standard Dutch exchange rate. The public association's pricing trend stabilized. Number 24 crude sugar white ex-warehouse bid remained at 15 taels, but sales were scarce. As today is Sunday, neither side relented, and no transactions occurred. Number 20 medium sugar discounted white was firm at 14 taels 4 qian, and Number 18 medium sugar white was firm at 14 taels 2 qian. Red sugar remained unchanged. Number 8 Dutch red was 11 taels 2 qian, unchanged. Number 90 Dutch red was 11 taels 5 qian to 11 taels 7 qian, slightly higher than the previous day. Chaozhou merchants opened a batch of white slices yesterday, totaling 50 bags, with a bright color, so the price opened at 10 taels, and the market looked good.

Sales of Min Bamboo Branches from Northern Jiangsu are Stagnant

Recently, very few Min bamboo branches have arrived. The previous arrivals still have some unopened batches because sales are exceptionally stagnant, and the arrivals are not pure. Therefore, the Jinshan branches have captured the market, and there is no hope for development. The current market price for higher-quality branches is no more than 20 taels, and there are few buyers. Only the Kuilan bamboo can still be sold, even with an increase of 8 or 9 taels, because both arrivals and inventory are scarce, but the quantity is limited.

Free Talk

Random Notes on the New Science of Augury by Zhan Lu

The science of augury, as told to me by history, could foretell the safety, danger, rise, and fall of nations, as well as the successes, failures, misfortunes, and blessings of individuals, based on the observation of atmospheric phenomena. What an amazing skill! Now, in modern times, we no longer hear of its successors. Could it be that the science of augury has been lost? Or was it originally a fabrication, with the ancients exaggerating in historical accounts?

In reality, there is now a new science of augury that everyone knows and understands. It is widespread, and simply opening the daily newspaper can serve as a tool to test this new science of augury.

Looking at the countries of Europe and America, one feels a sense of economic recession. The arrogance of one country affects the implementation of military reduction. The resentment of another country brews revenge. And the unwavering determination of a certain small South American country refuses to yield, all of which are manifestations of ominous signs. Even the United Kingdom and the United States, known for their wealth and power, have recently shown signs of economic recession. Look at the British Prince being ridiculed by unemployed and impoverished people during his travels. Look at the American President being subjected to all sorts of insults from the opposition during his speeches. What do these phenomena signify? Alas, it is self-evident!

An island nation embracing aggression appears outwardly to have the ambition to conquer the entirety of Manchuria. But wanting to "blow a breath to cook a cow's head," the problem has many aspects. As their own people say, swallowing Manchuria is like swallowing a bomb. When it explodes in the future, it may lead to their demise.

Looking back at our own country, the situation feels increasingly dire! All courage and heroic spirit have fled to the outside of the pass. Only the tearful and exhausted National Salvation Army and the volunteer forces are struggling and shouting there! Speaking of within the pass, the extravagance of important figures, the grievances of disaster victims, and the maliciousness of unscrupulous merchants have long created a chaotic and smoky atmosphere. To add to this, the troubles in Shandong have not ended, and the chaos in Sichuan has arisen again. They are very polite to foreign insults, but "attack each other with murderous intent" towards their own people. This is the bad luck of the people in the war zone! Alas, at this state of affairs, one's chest is truly bursting with anger.

Reading Wen Tianxiang's Song of Righteousness, many figures are described as having "righteousness that fills the mountains and rivers." Where have they all gone now? Righteous people cannot be found. The only thing that can be found is, as the people of Suzhou say: a crooked mouth blowing a trumpet, a bunch of evil energy.

Song of Winter Clothing! By Cheng Luding — Sung for all the gentlemen and ladies to hear —

Autumn has quietly departed, and winter has quietly arrived.

Red leaves and yellow flowers arranged the farewell feast of autumn; cold winds and severe frost prepared the fragrant carriage of winter.

The golden wind caresses the face, and the jade dew condenses into frost. This is precisely the time when autumn departs and winter arrives. Naturally, autumn has swept away a piece of my heart-stirring sorrow; indeed, winter has added a string of my heart-breaking tears!

Autumn departs and winter arrives. In this process, countless white hairs and rosy faces, one needle after another stringing together tear drops, one strand of sorrow after another, weave winter clothing, entrusting the migrating geese to bring to loved ones. However, in the broken mountains and rivers, there are also national heroes charging through blood and sleeping exposed with their spears as pillows. I cry, I grieve, but I truly do not wish to write anymore. On that line between life and death, what kind of world is it?

Ten thousand miles of desolate frontiers, thousands of lonely soldiers, the grass is exhausted, and the trees are gone; the rain weeps, and the wind howls; snowflakes and blood flowers fly wildly; the voices of ghosts and cries echo together. In this place, there is no warm and gentle place; there is no supply of fur coats and cotton clothing; there is only hot blood, only cold tears, only courage, only ambition to live through this bitter life of ice and snow.

If one has feelings, who would stand idly by? If one has reason, who would turn a blind eye? Unless one is a person with a mental disorder, who could bear to let them continue like this? Or, conversely, should one not make an effort to assist them?

The economy and food are certainly important, but the winter clothing they need now is also urgently needed. Conversely, their needs are our needs; their suffering is no different from our suffering!

Moreover, the survival or demise of a country must have its reasons for survival or demise, must have its possibilities for survival or demise, which depend on the will and actions of the people.

If China did not have them! Even if they existed, but without their will, without their actions, then China would have already perished. At most, it would only be a China that exists in name only.

The only thing that can allow China to seek survival from the brink of extinction is them, and only with them will it not perish.

This is not an exaggeration; this is not excessive praise; moreover, the ironclad facts are undeniable facts.

Gentlemen, ladies, having heard my Song of Winter Clothing, what should you do?

Not only what should you do! But also, you should come up with a solution.

Blue Sky, White Sun, Crimson Ground by Shen Yulin

During their schooling years, young people should exercise their bodies, concentrate on their studies, and build a solid foundation to become the masters of the future. Leaving school and serving the society and the people, one should not follow the crowd but should transform the adverse environment of society!

Never forget national humiliation every day until the day of avenging the humiliation arrives. Otherwise, living a life of pleasure and ignorance, the future of the country will be unimaginable!

Freely received, freely given away: this is the words and actions of Jesus Christ. If the world could see through everything, universal harmony could be achieved immediately!

Japanese imperialists are the common enemy of the Chinese people. If we do not have the ability to eliminate them, we simply have no days to live!

The Manchukuo puppet state! Any country that upholds justice will not recognize it because its organization is insidious and its background is vile! We should stand on the same battle line without delay to attack it!

The loss of territory is the ultimate shame and disgrace of a country! Actively recovering lost territory is the only path to survival for the Chinese nation!

Red blood, the blood must be hot. Taking advantage of the hot blood, go and annihilate the enemy! (Unpaid)

Modern Fable – A Felt Hat and Silk Stockings by Qian Xiao

When the modern young man was asleep. A felt hat on the coat rack laughed at a pair of silk stockings: "You are so lowly! You are only used to cover the feet and accompany leather shoes. As for me, I am high above, rubbing against the nicely combed hair. How pleasant!" The silk stockings had no words to answer his arrogant words.

A few days later, the young man felt that the felt hat on his head was no longer fashionable, so he sent it to the shoe store to be made into a pair of spats (worn over leather shoes when wearing a suit). At the same time, he cut off the leg of the silk stockings and made a delicate hairnet (modern young men often use discarded silk stockings to make hairnets) and put it on his head.

The hairnet looked down from his head and recognized that the felt spats on the young man's feet were the felt hat that had ridiculed him. So, he retaliated: "Felt hat, how come you are also covering the feet, and living a lowly life accompanying leather shoes?" The felt hat looked up and remembered that the hairnet was the silk stockings that he had mocked. He felt so ashamed that he could not find a place to hide.

The Chinese National Road Construction Association is holding its 12th anniversary exhibition and entertainment gathering at the New World. It started on October 8th and will last for one month. During this month, in addition to the dozen or so entertainment performances regularly staged by the New World, various special programs are also being rehearsed at the Xinhua Theater. In the coming half month, there are still many well-known non-professional entertainment groups that need to participate. Movie stars Zhang Zhiyun, Yang Naimei, and others will also perform innovative programs. It is also reported that well-known playwrights Tang Huaiqiu, Ying Yunwei, Yuan Muzhi, Meng Junmou, and Yan Gefan are organizing comrades to rehearse famous plays. The acting period has been scheduled for three days from the 29th to the 31st of the month. There are four plays on the program: (1) "The Boor" by Chekhov of Russia, (2) "After Drinking" by Ding Xilin, (3) "The Transaction" by Ouyang Yuqian, and (4) "Father Returns" by Kikuchi Kan of Japan. In addition to the above five people, Zhang Huiling, Ren Guang, Shen Tong, Qian Rulin, Rao Jianchang, Wang Xiawen, Wang Shaoqing, and Ms. Li Lilian, Wu Jiatang, Wang Ying, Tang Xiangqing, and Min Cuiying are also participating in the performance. It is said that the scenery and props are specially made. It is truly commendable to have such talent performing such famous plays.

Rotary Club Travelogue with the Postman into Guan (26) by Seeking Happiness Studio Owner

At this moment, the postmen broke free from the shackles of the Japanese and returned to being free citizens of the Republic of China. They saw the national flag that they had not seen for several days flying over the Shanhaiguan city gate! Each and every one of them was overjoyed and ecstatic, not knowing whether to laugh or cry! Lu Boqin firmly grasped Tong Yizhen's hand and loudly celebrated:

"We have safely entered Guan! From now on, there will only be eternal love, and there will be no obstacles or difficulties on our path of love!"

But at this moment, Tong Yizhen suddenly missed her homeland. In Lu Boqin's arms, she sweetly sobbed and said, "Although I have found a lover, I don't necessarily miss my hometown. However, the Northeast is still the territory of the Republic of China, and the people of the Northeast are still the people of the Republic of China! Thinking that the place is now forcibly occupied by the brutal Japanese, and the people are all prisoners, I don't know when it will be recovered? When will we be free? If there is no possibility of recovery for a long time, I will never have hope of returning home. How can I not cry bitterly?"

Lu Boqin fell silent again upon hearing this! After a long daze, he could not think of any words to comfort Yizhen. They arrived in Beiping feeling depressed and unhappy.

After getting off the train in Beiping, he took Yizhen directly to his cousin Lu Danian's house, explained everything, and Lu Danian readily agreed, allowing them to stay at his house and promising to complete their wedding ceremony on a selected date. Lu Boqin also received a notice from the post office that he had been reassigned to work at the Beiping General Post Office, so the problem of livelihood was not a concern.

One day, the Beiping Post Office held a special welcome party for their comrades from the Northeast. Lu Boqin was running around the venue when he suddenly heard an old colleague making behind-the-back sarcastic remarks about him in front of others:

"Only Little Lu is doing well. During the national crisis and when all of us are suffering, he even managed to seduce a beautiful wife." It turned out that now that they had reached a peaceful state, they could discuss right and wrong and settle old scores again!

But Lu Boqin seemed to have heard a loud thunderclap and was sweating profusely and feeling very uneasy. Before the meeting ended, he hurried home and told his cousin and Yizhen everything he had heard today. He then resolutely put forward a firm proposal:

"Who knew that I still avoid being unscrupulous! But I am definitely not a heartless person and should always find a way to correct it. From now on, I will go to the post office to work, and Yizhen will go to school wholeheartedly. The wedding will not be held for the time being. It must wait until the Northeast is recovered before it can be celebrated, so as to avoid others from criticizing me for only knowing personal love. Alas! How can there be a home before the Northeast is recovered! I should be the first to worry about the world and the last to enjoy it, striving to be an ordinary person with a responsibility for the rise and fall of the country!"

So, Lu Danian and Tong Yizhen both lowered their heads and remained silently facing each other. ?

The end of this novel is only that uncertain question mark in the small title on the right. When will the Northeast be recovered? When will this loving couple get married? Or will the Northeast never be recovered? Will they never get married? Or will there be other changes and transformations? Let's treat them all as long-standing problems for now. (The End)

Lin Sen Returns to Nanjing Tomorrow

▲ Reorganization of Fujian Province Nears Completion

▲ Chiang Kwang-nai to Serve as Chairman

According to the Kwok Man News Agency, after National Government Chairman Lin Sen returned to Shanghai from Fujian, reporters learned that Lin has decided to return to Nanjing tomorrow (31st) morning. Only Lin Chi-tang will accompany him. When reporters asked someone close to Lin about the reorganization of the Fujian provincial government, they were told that Chiang Kwang-nai and Tsai Ting-kai had previously met Lin in Shanghai to discuss the reorganization of the provincial government. Later, Chiang flew to Hankou to see Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. At that time, Chiang Kai-shek also said that the reorganization of Fujian Province was indeed necessary, but after the reorganization, Chiang Kwang-nai must preside over the position of chairman. At the time, Chiang (Kwang-nai) believed that unifying the Fujian army and breaking the separatist situation was his duty, but he felt that he was a soldier and not suited for politics, and he declined the position in person. As a result of the meeting, Chiang (Kwang-nai) only agreed to go to Fujian to take a look before making a decision. Now that Chen Kuo-yao has been resolved and the Fujian Communists in Longyan have been defeated, the reorganization of the Fujian provincial government is inevitable. After several telegraphic discussions, it has now become concrete. It is said that Chiang Kwang-nai has also agreed to serve as chairman. As for the provincial committee, Tsai Ting-kai, Sun Hsi-wen, and Fan Chi-wu have been internally determined. Once Chiang Kwang-nai sends another telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in Hankou, the official announcement can be made. The above are all past and recent facts.

Municipal Government Rehabilitation Bonds

▲ Under Negotiation with Shanghai Banking Syndicate

▲ Secured by Wharf Dues

The Municipal Government has decided to issue six million yuan in rehabilitation bonds to rebuild the Zhabei war zone. This matter was stated to the China Eastern News Agency reporter by Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hung-chun yesterday. The matter is currently being discussed by Municipal Finance Bureau Director Tsai Tseng-chi and a certain banking syndicate. Once finalized, all bonds will be entrusted to the banking syndicate for safekeeping. Whether they will be circulated in the market will be decided by the banking syndicate itself. Currently, the Municipal Government plans to mortgage the bonds at 80% of their face value and stipulates that no kickbacks can be deducted to ensure that all proceeds are used for public purposes. The security for these bonds is the entire income from wharf dues, which will be repaid over 20 years. The Municipal Government can obtain at least 600,000 yuan annually from wharf dues, so the security is extremely secure. Furthermore, the regulations for these bonds have been submitted by the Municipal Government to the central government for approval and filing.

Wang Pei-yuan Discusses Inspecting Disaster Conditions in Northeast China

▲ and Will Depart for the Philippines Tomorrow

▲ to Attend the Inauguration Ceremony of the Local Red Cross Society Branch

According to the Central News Agency, Wang Pei-yuan, Chairman of the Chinese Red Cross Society, went to Northeast China to inspect the disaster situation and seek relief. He returned to Shanghai yesterday. He stated that various charitable organizations in the city, in view of the severity of the disaster in Northeast China and the urgent need for relief, commissioned him to go north to negotiate with charitable organizations in the north. A decision has been made and has been telegraphed by the Chinese Red Cross Society to the International Red Cross Society, requesting that the Japanese authorities be notified not to obstruct it. As soon as a reply is received, personnel will be dispatched to work. 300,000 yuan has already been raised for the necessary expenses. Wang also told reporters that he is scheduled to depart for the Philippines tomorrow (31st) to represent the Chinese Red Cross Society in attending the inauguration ceremony of the American Red Cross Society's Philippine branch building and will also need to discuss everything with the local Red Cross Society.

Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee Held Its Tenth Regular Board Meeting Yesterday

▲ Discussions on the Iron Department Loan to be Held Tomorrow

The Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee held its tenth regular board meeting at 10:00 AM yesterday on the fourth floor of the Bank Association on Hong Kong Road to discuss committee affairs. In addition to discussing ways to subsidize educational and cultural undertakings and deciding to hold a general meeting tomorrow to discuss the Iron Department's loan, it also planned to hold a discussion meeting today.

▲ Attendees: Those who attended the board meeting yesterday morning included Vice Chairman Mr. Massyke of the United Kingdom, Director Yeh Kung-cho, Liu Jui-heng, Tseng Yung-fu, and Secretary General Hang Li-wu. Chairman Chu Chia-hua did not arrive in time due to the train not running yesterday morning and was temporarily replaced by the vice chairman. Director Yen Te-ching of China and Director Brown of the United Kingdom were both absent and were temporarily replaced by Liu Jui-heng and Massyke. The meeting lasted approximately two hours and adjourned around 12:00 PM.

▲ Meeting Results: During the meeting, in addition to reporting on committee affairs, there was a detailed discussion on subsidizing educational and cultural undertakings. The committee plans to use the hundreds of thousands of yuan in interest held by the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Purchasing Committee in London at HSBC to subsidize educational and cultural undertakings. However, after inquiring with London, there has been no satisfactory reply. It has been decided to temporarily seek assistance from private sources, that is, to telegraph our country's Minister to London Kuo Tai-chi to contact the committee and expedite the transfer of funds to Shanghai.

▲ Loan Issue: Secretary General Hang Li-wu stated that the Iron Department's loan issue has been approved for discussion at the general meeting tomorrow. On one hand, the Minister of Railways Ku Meng-yu has been telegraphed to send representatives to Shanghai to provide detailed explanations to the committee. The loan is related to the completion of the Yuehan Railway and involves the issuance of 40 million yuan in bonds by the Ministry of Railways, secured by the committee's funds. The loan to complete the Tongguan-Xi'an section of the Longhai Railway is 500,000 pounds, approximately 9 million yuan in Chinese currency.

▲ Discussion Meeting: The Iron Department's loan issue is of utmost importance, and the discussion time must be a full day. For the convenience of discussion, the committee plans to hold a discussion meeting today to exchange views first, but the time and location have not been determined.

Italian Party Celebrates Tenth Anniversary

▲ Count Ciano and Count Bono both gave speeches

According to the North China Daily News, yesterday (28th) was the tenth anniversary of the Italian Fascist Party's March on Rome. Italian expatriates in the city went to the residence of Italian Minister Count Ciano at 555 Jing'an Temple Road to celebrate. Those affiliated with the Fascist Party all went in black shirts. The Italian Minister gave a speech, recounting the progress of Italy under Mussolini's leadership, especially the progress in adjusting labor-management relations. The so-called Labor Charter can be used as a model for other countries in the future. Therefore, the trust in the Fascist Party by compatriots at home and abroad has rapidly increased. After the Italian Envoy finished speaking, the audience applauded thunderously, and all listeners were moved. They then sang the party song and dispersed. Domestic Term Deposit Interest Rate Set 115

—Price at 5 Taels and 5 Mace—

The current term delivery situation is far less prosperous than in previous years. Term lending is even more indifferent, simply regarded as if nothing were happening. Only term deposit interest rates remain undiminished, as there is no other safe place for wealthy households to store their silver and money besides the deposit business. Therefore, the amount of term deposits remains unchanged from the past. As for the term deposit interest rate, it has always been determined by discussions among senior money industry members, observing market conditions, and the overall trend of supply and demand. This term could have been reduced due to a lack of demand, but it was still decided to be 5 taels and 5 mace, with little difference from the previous term (April)'s market price, in order to prevent unforeseen circumstances and maintain relationships with wealthy households.

The Entire Process and Delivery Situation of Yarn and Cotton This Month 119

▲People's Labeled Yarn: The rise and fall of People's labeled yarn in October was extremely significant. It entered the market in mid-May, priced around 155 taels, reaching a high of 57 taels. Subsequently, due to the decline of rural areas domestically, financial depression, and sluggish actual demand, it fell below the 40-tael mark, to 138 taels. Then, Rong Xing Company (榮興號) took the opportunity to switch from short to long positions, and market sentiment gradually improved. At the same time, the Cantonese group in the southern port actively purchased, and in July and August, spot yarn sales reached approximately 100,000 bales. As a result, market inventory was scarce, and various factories opened large short positions in futures, making the market more stable. Unexpectedly, the US cotton government estimate was released on August 8, showing a decrease in production, jumping over 80 pounds, which greatly boosted sentiment, breaking through the 50-tael mark. However, US cotton continued to rise, and the upward trend was unstoppable. The highest spot price reached 9.2 cents. As for the short positions, they were quite uneasy and had to painfully close their positions. The highest price seen was over 158 taels. However, although the rise was strong, customer demand was not strong, which made the market less than perfect. The US cotton second estimate on September 8 showed a slight increase of 4,000 bales, and the market price plummeted by over 100 pounds. This greatly disappointed the buyers and fell below the 50-tael mark. The sellers' momentum grew stronger day by day, with heavy pressure. Yongan Company's (永安) long positions struggled desperately, but the environment was too bad, and conflicts occurred in Sichuan and Shandong provinces. The US cotton situation was also weak and depressed, and various groups did not purchase spot yarn. Some retail investors, seeing the poor surrounding atmosphere, closed their positions slightly. The lowest price seen in mid-October was 142 taels and 6 qian. The general market target was to see if the 40-tael mark could be maintained. It was said that the sellers had a large amount of goods to deliver, and Rong Xing's long positions were preparing to buy in the difficulties. Therefore, until the last day, the delivery was slightly short, and the scattered short positions covered their positions, and the market rose sharply. It rose by 3 taels and 1 qian in one day, with the last transaction at 146 taels. However, it was 5 taels lower than the price in the previous month. As a result, 11,600 bales remained, of which 6,750 bales were for self-delivery, and another 4,350 bales were for actual delivery. It is estimated that 2,550 bales of 20-count people's clock yarn, 700 bales of Songhe, 350 bales of Dragon Boat, 350 bales of Caihua, and 400 bales of Baoyi were delivered. The delivery price was 144 taels. Yongan Factory was the only buyer. The delivery side was also guaranteed by Bao's manufacturers and Shao. The initial strong momentum was completely dispersed, with a sharp drop of 1 tael and 5 qian. The Ningbo group also sold out, and the sellers took the opportunity to pursue, but the buyers never released the amount they bought. As for the sellers, they were also determined not to resist the advance. Most people looked at 30 taels to enter customs, so both the long and short sides had considerable strength. Worldly Morals Decline, Alas, the Death of a Girl 125

Hong Ding, courtesy name Zhenjiu, a native of Shouxian County, Anhui, residing at No. 16 Yongqing Lane, Beile Road, French Concession, was 49 years old and worked in a certain party headquarters. His wife, Wu, was 33 years old. Because they had no daughters, they adopted their younger brother's daughter, Xiuying, as their adopted daughter. Last night, at around 10:00 PM, the girl felt hungry and asked her mother for six copper coins to go out and buy steamed buns to fill her stomach. Unexpectedly, after going out, she was lured to a certain place by criminals and forcibly raped. After the incident, the rapist fled. At around 11:00 PM, the girl still bought steamed buns and returned home. Her mother thought that the child was playing outside and did not expect an accident, so she did not ask her how long she had been out or what had happened. After the girl finished eating the steamed buns, the mother and daughter went to bed together. At this time, Hong was out attending a banquet with friends and had not returned. At 2:00 AM, Hong returned and knocked on the door. When the girl got up to open the door, Hong caught a glimpse of blood flowing from her legs. When asked, she did not understand why. He immediately ordered his wife to investigate. Wu discovered that the child's lower private parts were bleeding. Shocked, she sternly questioned her. The girl then told her mother what had happened, but there was no way to find the criminal. She was immediately sent to a small hospital on South Chengdu Road for treatment and returned home, but the bleeding did not stop. She was sent to the hospital again for treatment. The doctor replied that the hospital was not equipped and could not start treatment, and instructed her to send her to a large hospital. At this point, Hong and his wife sent the girl to Renji Hospital for treatment at 6:15 AM yesterday morning. After examination by the doctor, it was found that the internal blood vessels were ruptured due to injury. Surgery was performed immediately, but due to the severity of the injury, the treatment was ineffective, and she died at 12:30 PM yesterday afternoon. The hospital reported to the French Concession Xiafei Police Station as usual and sent detectives to investigate. The body was sent to the Tongren Fuyuan branch for examination, awaiting a report to the Second Special Court for personnel to examine the body.

Continued Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Workers Pass Through Shanghai to Hangzhou 126

The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Engineering Office sent personnel to recruit 3,000 workers in places such as Beijing and Tianjin. The first batch of workers, totaling 213, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and were transferred to Hangzhou by the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway train. Yesterday, the second batch of workers, totaling about 300, arrived from Tianjin on the Lisheng Steamer (利生輪船). They arrived at the South Station at 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon. The foreman, Hua Baomin, contacted the South Station Chief of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, presented his passport, and requested five cars. He then left for Changshan at 9:25 PM that night, attached to the No. 406 night freight train. It is reported that more than 2,000 people will continue to arrive in Shanghai and transfer to Hangzhou.

Case of Abduction and Trafficking of a Young Girl Involves a Foreigner.

A Foreigner Must Be Brought to Court for Further Interrogation.

The Sequence of Events Is Untrue and Incomplete.

Wu Zhu, a woman from Wuxi residing at No. 811, Baidang Road, French Concession, is 49 years old. She used to work as a servant for foreigners. She has a daughter named A Bao, who is 18 years old and already betrothed to someone. Suddenly, in April of this year, A Bao was abducted and went missing. After being found and brought back, she ran away again. It was not until now that it was discovered she had been abducted and hidden by Feng Abing, a Shaoxing native hired by the police. Wu Zhu hired lawyer Dong Qian to report the case to the French police, who dispatched Detective Shen Jinfu to first arrest Feng. Then, while arresting Wu A Bao, they happened to encounter her on Fuli Li Road and brought her to the police station together. Yesterday, they were escorted to the Second Special District Court for investigation. Wang Gangxu, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division, took his seat in the First Criminal Court to conduct the trial. First, Yuan Jiahan, the police lawyer, stated the case and filed charges according to Article 257 of the Criminal Law. Then, Detective Shen Jinfu reported the circumstances of the arrest of the defendant. Next, the plaintiff, Wu Zhu, stated, "A Bao is my biological daughter, 18 years old this year, born on December 16th of the Republic of China's 4th year, zodiac Rabbit. She used to work in a cigarette factory and is already betrothed to someone, with the wedding set for October 18th. Unexpectedly, she was abducted in April, and it has now been discovered that she was abducted and hidden by the defendant. I reported the case to the police and requested an investigation." Lawyer Dong Yu, representing the plaintiff, requested to file a private prosecution and demanded that the defendant hand over the person, and so on. The judge ordered Feng to be taken down and first interrogated Wu A Bao. Wu stated, "Wu Zhu is my mother. I don't know if she is my biological mother. Zhou Shengyuan introduced me to Feng. First, he introduced me to a foreigner at No. 14 for 50 yuan a month, giving 30 yuan to my mother and 20 yuan to me. After two months, the foreigner didn't want me anymore. Then, Zhou introduced me to Feng Abing, and we lived together from May 2nd. It was agreed that Feng would give me 10 yuan a month. The first month's money was given to Zhou to be passed on to my mother, and the second month's money I gave to my mother myself. In August, I didn't have money to give to my mother because I was giving birth, so I left Feng. My mother knew everything that happened." Feng Abing confessed that he was 22 years old and Zhou Shengyuan introduced A Bao to live with him, and the rest of his statement was the same as Wu's. The judge then questioned Wu Zhu, who claimed that she did not know about her daughter's affairs outside and did not receive any money. The witness, Zhou Shengyuan, testified that he knew Wu Zhu and slightly knew Feng. "I did not introduce A Bao to the foreigner or to live with Feng. However, A Bao was betrothed to Gui Xinggen, and I was the matchmaker. Since I was the matchmaker for Gui, how could I introduce A Bao to someone else? I have been falsely accused and request an investigation." The judge then asked A Bao who she wished to live with. A Bao replied that living with Feng was not a long-term plan and she wished to go home with her mother and marry a proper husband. At this point, the judge ruled that the case involved a foreigner who had not been brought to court and adjourned the hearing to November 2nd for further interrogation. The defendants were returned to custody, and the detective in charge of the case was ordered to invite the foreigner to court for questioning next time. The defense lawyer for the defendant requested bail, but the court denied it.

▲ Many Proposals Submitted to the Executive Committee for Discussion and Implementation

The China Benevolent Childcare Association held its fourth annual semi-annual meeting yesterday at 3:00 PM at the Bank Club on Hong Kong Road. There were 53 proposals for discussion, and the event was well-attended, making it a grand occasion. The details are as follows:

▲ Attendees Present included Li Zhaohuan, President of Jiaotong University, representing Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau; Chen Lengseng of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau; Chen Heqin, Director of the Chinese Church of the Shanghai Municipal Council; Liu Zhanen, President of Shanghai University; Weng Guoxun of Minfu School; Tan Bozhi of the YMCA; and association staff Liu Liming, Wu Weide, Chen Tiesheng, Hu Xuanming, Hu Zhou Shuan, Yu Xuanxuan, Wang Zhian, etc., along with foreign guests, totaling over 60 people. (8) Dr. Hu Xuanming announced the proposals (summary excerpt below). (9) Guest Speeches: (A) Chen Lengseng spoke on "Love Your Children and Extend That Love to Others' Children." (B) Weng Guoxun spoke on "Children's Occupations and Banning Children from Pulling Carts." (C) Tan Bozhi spoke on "Promoting Benevolent Childcare Work." The meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM.

▲ Work Report Secretary-General Wu Weide reported on the semi-annual work summary: (A) Under General Affairs: The National Government allocated over 20 acres of government land for the base of the Nanjing Model Education Center. (B) Under Child Protection: (1) 21 cases of relief were implemented in the local area; (2) Relief was implemented in three cases in other areas, including Wuxian, Zhuji, Zhejiang, and Changsha, Hunan. Under the Maladjusted Children's Education Department: (1) Regarding the Shanghai Benevolent Childcare Education Center; (2) Regarding the Shanghai Municipal Disaster Relief Shelter's Childcare Group; (3) Regarding the Shanghai War Zone Orphans Temporary Education Center; (4) Operating the Wuhan Flood Orphans Temporary Relief Center. (D) Under the Child Health Department: (1) Zhabei Benevolent Childcare Health Clinic; (2) Yangshupu Benevolent Childcare Health Clinic; (3) Examining the health of children at the Shanghai Benevolent Childcare Education Center and the Shanghai War Zone Temporary Education Center. (E) Under the Child Research Department: (1) Overview of the Benevolent Childcare Garden; (2) Mrs. Hu Xuanming, a member of the association, edited a collection of children's songs; (3) Wang Zhian, secretary of the association, edited the History of Chinese Children and Biographies of Wise Mothers in Chinese Dynasties.

▲ Summary of Proposals According to Dr. Hu Xuanming's report, the semi-annual meeting received 53 proposals, none of which were identical. It was decided to transfer them to the Executive Committee for discussion and implementation.

Dr. Lu Shoushan Commits Suicide by Swallowing Opium

Lu Shoushan, a 64-year-old Cantonese man, resided in the kitchen of No. 491, Dexing Lane, Peng Road, and practiced medicine there. For unknown reasons, he committed suicide by swallowing opium the other day. His cohabitant, Li Jingming, discovered this and immediately reported it to the Hongkou Police Station, which ordered detectives to go to the scene and send him to Tongren Hospital for treatment. He died soon after. The body was taken to the postmortem examination facility on Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court dispatched Prosecutor Guo Wei to the facility to examine the body. According to Li Jingming, who is 22 years old and cohabited with the deceased, around 7:00 PM the day before, a patient came to the doctor's office seeking treatment. However, the doctor was groaning in bed and refused to see the patient despite being called. Hearing the noise, Li went to check and found something amiss, so he reported it to the police, and so on. According to the deceased's son, Lu Binggan, who is 22 years old and works as a clerk in a leather shoe store at No. 186 Sichuan Road, the deceased was his father. He was at the store that day and did not know what happened. His father had a cough, and his medical career was not bad, so the reason for his suicide may have been due to illness. After receiving the testimony, Mr. Guo ruled that the deceased, Lu Shoushan, a male, died by poisoning himself before death. The body was handed over to his son, Lu Binggan, who signed a document to take it back for coffin and burial.

Female Corpse in West Shanghai Examined and Found to Have Died from Poisoning

Regarding the case of the bizarre discovery of a young woman's body in a pavilion room on the top floor of No. 13, Jinjia Lane, near Kangjia Bridge on Jisi Feier Road in West Shanghai, the details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. After the incident, the deceased's younger brother, Qin Shiwu, rushed to the scene. He claimed that his sister (i.e., the woman) was 23 years old this year, and her relationship with her husband had always been very good. They were inseparable. Recently, due to her husband's unemployment, their finances had become strained, leading to frequent arguments. His sister had a pretty face and a petite figure, and she usually dressed very meticulously. The local security chief of the 12th District, Shen Qi, reported the case to the local court the afternoon before. Yesterday morning at 11:00 AM, Prosecutor Cao Changlin was dispatched by the court, along with the coroner, to the scene. The examination revealed that the female corpse's hair was disheveled, and her head was swollen to the size of a bucket. Her entire body was bloated, emitting a foul odor. Both legs were swollen like giant logs, and her back was black. Blood was flowing from her mouth, and her tongue was protruding from her lips. She was wearing a blue-striped cotton shirt, covered with a green and red-edged woolen vest, blue-striped cotton shorts, and was barefoot. There were no injuries. It was confirmed that she died from poisoning. The deceased's younger brother, Tai Shiwu, signed a document to prepare a coffin for burial. Inspector Li Yuanduo from the Public Security Bureau arrived at the scene to investigate. He noted that the bedding on the shop was neatly arranged, and there were several pieces of clothing hanging on the clothes rack. Torn pieces of the woman's photo were scattered on the floor. The cause of death was difficult to determine at the moment and would only be clear after her husband, Zhang Zhenyuan, was apprehended. It was also heard that the sub-landlord, Wang Abing, received an anonymous letter with the words "Public Health Bureau" on it, which was quite ridiculous.

First Special District Court Burns Confiscated Drugs

The Shanghai First Special District Court regularly publicly burns confiscated opium, red pills, morphine, cocaine, heroin, and other types of drugs every three months to eliminate the poisonous atmosphere. The drugs confiscated in July, August, and September are now stored in the contraband warehouse in large quantities. After approval from the Ministry of Judicial Administration, the court, led by President Zhou and Chief Prosecutor Wang, followed the established procedure and chose the Yizuka land of the Bao'an Hall on the south side of the court as the burning site. Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, court clerks were ordered to move all the drugs that had been definitively judged in court from the warehouse to the Yizuka land. Under the supervision of the assigned prosecutor, the opium and red pills were thrown into the flames one by one, and a large amount of kerosene was poured on them to ensure they were completely reduced to ashes. During the burning, in addition to the meticulous work of the prosecutors, judicial police, and clerks dispatched by the court, the Shanghai Municipal Council and the Law Society also sent representatives to the scene to observe.

Rental Reduction Issue in Baoyu Lane

▲ Landlord Agrees to Cancel the 5 Yuan Rent Increase

Tenants in Baoyu Lane, Caishi Street, French Concession, face a dire situation as their residences stand largely vacant, with nine out of ten units empty. Since the outbreak of war, they have been forced to pawn and borrow to pay their monthly rent, accumulating insurmountable debts. Many tenants are several months behind on their rent, and over ten households have been sued in court by the landlord, facing imminent ruin. Therefore, they earnestly requested the landlord, Dehe Foreign Firm, to consider their plight and reduce the rent by 20-30% to maintain the status quo. Upon receiving the letter, Dehe Foreign Firm immediately dispatched senior foreign staff the next day to conduct a door-to-door survey in Baoyu Lane, confirming the high vacancy rate. Subsequently, they sent representative Chen Guansheng to hold a negotiation meeting with tenant representatives at No. 30 Baoyu Lane on the afternoon of the day before. Tenant representatives included Yao Zhaoji, Yao Shouren, Zou Fengshan, Yao Wenqing, Tang Yinyuan, etc. As a result of the negotiations, the landlord representative firmly refused to reduce the rent. After tenant representative Mr. Yao and others explained the plight of the tenants, emphasizing that it would be difficult to sustain without a rent reduction, the landlord representative, Mr. Chen, only agreed to cancel the 5-yuan rent increase per building starting from November, but remained firm on not reducing the rent. The tenant representatives argued that with the current economic downturn, the existing rent was already a heavy burden, and a further increase would be unbearable. They believed that the benevolent landlord would not resort to such measures and implored Mr. Chen to convey their plea to the landlord, emphasizing that they were long-term tenants who were on the brink of bankruptcy due to the current difficulties and requested a rent reduction to maintain the status quo. Representative Chen still refused to accept, only agreeing to cancel the proposed 5-yuan rent increase. The tenant representatives, considering the interests of all tenants in the lane, agreed to convene a meeting of all tenants to seek public opinion and respond in writing. The meeting adjourned at 10:00 PM.

Female Tea Room Attendant and Fish Stall Owner

▲ Initial Union Was Illicit

▲ Sudden Falling Out Leads to Legal Dispute

Tai Afeng, a charming tea attendant in her twenties at the Tianyun Teahouse in the Yong'an Company amusement park, is known for her attentive service to guests. Two years ago, Fei Ahua, a fish stall owner from Ningbo in the Hongkou market, visited the amusement park and met Afeng at the Tianyun Teahouse. Captivated by her beauty, he frequented the place and, over time, developed a close relationship with her. Despite being over forty, Fei, unaware of his age, believed he had won her favor and expressed his desire to take her as a concubine. Afeng initially pretended to agree, drawn by his wealth. Later, Fei moved her to No. 6, Baokang Lane, Zhejiang Road, due to the cramped living conditions at her previous address in Hongfu Lane, Xinzha Road. Afeng seized the opportunity to acquire a large sum of money to furnish the new residence. However, once her desires were fulfilled, she turned against Fei, treating him like a stranger. Angered, Fei reported to the Hongkou Police Station the night before, claiming that 875 yuan in cash, usually kept in an iron box at his wife's residence, had disappeared. He suspected Afeng had stolen the money, as the box was placed behind the chamber pot, unknown to anyone except Afeng, who could have seen it while visiting their house. The police dispatched detectives Zhang Faxiang and Liu Decheng to arrest Afeng at the Tianyun Teahouse and search her home, where they found 200 yuan in cash and three receipts. One receipt was for a copper bed priced at 155 yuan, another for various furniture items priced at 105 yuan, and the third for clothing materials priced at 75 yuan. Yesterday morning, Qin Afeng was escorted to the First Special District Court, where Judge Huang presided over the trial. The police lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, stated that the case was being prosecuted under Article 337 of the Criminal Law for theft. Fei Ahua then described the theft, stating that the exact date was uncertain, but it was around the 10th of this month. The defendant had visited his house, and since his wife and he were at the Hongkou market, the defendant, being a friend of his wife, often came and went. When questioned, Qin Afeng denied the theft and recounted her relationship with Fei since they met. Finally, the plaintiff's lawyer, Fan Gang, and the defendant's lawyer debated, and Judge Huang ordered Qin Afeng to be detained pending sentencing.

Three Cases of Rape Sentenced

▲ Sentenced to Ten Years of Imprisonment

Tang A'er, on the 9th of this month, at 6:00 PM, lured Gu Rulin's eleven-year-old daughter, A'fu, from No. 18, Dexing Lane, Xixin Bridge Street, French Concession, and at 3:00 AM that night, forcibly raped her near a trash can in Baoxing Lane. After the sentencing, the defendant was returned to the detention center to await the appeal period before being sent to prison.

Spectacular Summerling Peck Dance and Music Concert

▲ Professor and Queen

The music and dance concert to be held at Summerling Peck on November 3rd is reportedly organized by Professor Hughes-Lin of the National Conservatory of Music. The content is said to be both visually and aurally stunning. Professor Hughes-Lin is a master of music and has long been renowned both domestically and internationally. Since arriving in Shanghai, he has been hired as a specialized professor of instruments and singing at the National Conservatory of Music. Outside of classes, he has also organized the "Art Goddess Troupe" to specialize in the study of music and dance. Its nature is similar to our country's national theater troupe. The troupe is full of talent, all of whom are music and dance experts in Shanghai, but they never easily show their talents. The music and dance concert to be held this time was commissioned by the Chinese People's Livelihood Self-Help Society, and because it is a charitable cause, they finally agreed. However, the professor takes his responsibility very seriously and has put a lot of thought into the selection of performers. On the one hand, it is necessary to show the splendor of the "Art Goddess Troupe," and on the other hand, it is necessary to cater to the audience's tastes. Many of the troupe members are from Germany, Italy, and Russia, and it is difficult to find a pure English singer. Fortunately, Bai Ersha, the Shanghai Russian Queen who left Shanghai more than two years ago, suddenly returned from her travels. The professor immediately approached her to discuss it, and Ms. Bai immediately agreed. Thus, the program was finalized. In addition to singing, there will also be Miss Yuan Ruoyu's modern dance and the crystal of art dance, Summerling Peck Dance, among other types, which are especially novel in Shanghai. The tickets for the two daytime shows have reportedly been nearly sold out, and the two shows at 7:00 PM and 9:00 PM at night will be on pre-sale at Summerling Peck on Tuesday. Those who buy tickets will surely be extremely enthusiastic.

China Publishing Monthly Published

In recent years, many new books have been published, but there is no detailed statistical method to introduce them. Scholars cannot buy the books they want to read, and publishers cannot widely promote them. The Hangzhou Private Zhejiang Circulation Library, in view of this, has specially published the "China Publishing Monthly," which collects new books published by bookstores across the country and compiles them into a book using scientific methods to introduce them to middle schools and above schools, libraries, and party and government agencies across the country, which is truly good news. The first issue of the publication has already been published. In addition to introducing new books published across the country, it also includes the sections "Education News," "Library News," and "Literature and Art." The article "Humble Proposals for Improving Chinese School Education" by Mr. Cheng Tianfang, Director of the Zhejiang Education Department, is an especially valuable treatise. It is heard that each issue of the publication sells for 1 jiao, and a subscription for all twelve issues of the year is 1 yuan. The Shanghai Postal Workers' Union Library, No. 230 Laobazi Road, also sells the publication on consignment.

The Third Issue of Book Review Published

The Book Review Monthly, edited by Professor Liu Yingshi, has published articles that have been carefully selected and include real names to indicate responsibility since its publication, so it has gained the trust of readers, who regard it as a compass for purchasing and reading books. The third issue has now been published ahead of schedule, and the content is richer than the previous issues. In addition to maintaining the original brilliance of the book review section, it also includes "The Unsuccessful Map of China" by Zhang Qiyun, a scholar of human geography, as the starting point for the publication's work on reviewing maps. In order to increase readers' interest, the publication has also added a new communications column. This issue includes letters from Luo Jialun, the president of Zhongda University, and others.

Recent News from the Guanshengyuan Catering Branch

The Guanshengyuan Catering Department of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce National Goods Mall has been open for half a month, and business is booming. In recent days, the number of men and women who have come to eat snacks has been endless, with shoulders rubbing against shoulders, and there are almost no empty seats. In order to reward the patronage, the manager of the department has specially reduced the prices, especially the prices of the company's main dishes and Guangzhou noodles, etc., which are the cheapest.

The Great Northeast Ocean United Price Reduction for Twenty-One Days

The Zhuangyuan Dakou Datong Hosiery Store and the Huaji Road Intersection Beiyang Hosiery Factory in Hongkou have been open for many years and have never reduced prices. This time, it is the eighth anniversary, and they are jointly reducing prices for twenty-one days starting on the 12th of this month, selling various goods at a loss.

Dehua Trading Company's Paint Sells Well

The Dehua Trading Company at No. 9 Fuzhou Road in Shanghai has been established for many years and has an excellent reputation. The Aiqi paint from the German Dada Paint Factory, managed by the company, has many colors, is excellent in quality, and beautiful in appearance, and is especially welcomed by all sectors of society. Now, in order to facilitate users, it has specially established a standard paint company to paint on behalf of customers. All parts can be painted on behalf of customers.

Tianlu Washington Shoe Store Price Reduction is Coming to an End

Since the Tianlu Shoe Store and Washington Shoe Store in Pontang Lane held a joint price reduction on the 12th of this month, all goods have been particularly cheap, and there is a new type of lightweight patterned leather shoe with a beautiful style and good quality, which is also being reduced in price along with the other goods. The price reduction is coming to an end, which is truly a great opportunity to buy shoes.

Hemorrhoid Expert Will Come to Shanghai

Mr. Fu Youqing, a Shandong hemorrhoid medical expert and president of Tianjin Renji Hospital, uses ancient Chinese methods to remove hemorrhoid roots for the treatment of hemorrhoids, without any pain. He is proficient in the skills of Hua Tuo, who was skilled in removing hemorrhoids, and Yuan Hua, who was skilled in extracting accumulations, and has reached a miraculous level. This time, he was invited by Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi to go to Guilin for diagnosis and treatment. He passed through Shanghai on the way. The patients in the region tried their best to keep him to treat hemorrhoids. Those who have been treated by him can eat, live, and live as normal people after the operation, which is especially rare. Mr. Fu will pass through Shanghai from Guilin soon, and it is said that he intends to stay for a short time to relieve the suffering of those with the same illness.

The Efficacy of Zhu Shaoyun's Scrofula Pills

Dr. Zhu Shaoyun, of Qinghefang, Zhejiang Road, invented Scrofula Pills, which have been around for more than 40 years. They are effective in treating various types of scrofula. All those who suffer from cervical tuberculosis, with sore and painful lumps, redness, swelling, and ulceration, can take them, and the efficacy is very effective.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather around Shandong is sunny with gentle northwesterly winds. The coastal area and the Yangtze River basin here are cloudy with fog or drizzle. The wind direction is uncertain and gentle. The weather south of Ma'an Island is cloudy with local rain, and the northeasterly wind is quite strong. The weather in the western part of Dongsha Island is very bad, with the center of the hurricane at 6:00 AM in the vicinity of the intersection of 21 degrees north latitude and 116 degrees east longitude, moving northwest-west. The wind force is unknown. Also, within 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 73.4 degrees and the lowest was 57.0 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 67.5 degrees and the lowest was 37.2 degrees.

National General Assembly of the Young Women's Christian Association Scheduled 130

▲ August 27 to September 4, Year 22

The National Young Women's Christian Association of China is required to hold a National General Assembly once every three years to gather ideas and determine important work guidelines. The Third National General Assembly has already been decided by the National Association's Annual Meeting to be held next year. Yesterday, the association held an Executive Committee meeting and discussed it in detail. It has been decided that it will be held in Peiping from August 27 to September 4 next year (Year 22). A Preparatory Committee was immediately elected to be responsible for discussing various matters of the General Assembly. The following were elected as members: Mrs. Wang Ziwne, Mrs. Ling Qijun, Dr. Xiang Maoying, Ms. Wu Yifang, Ms. Zeng Baosun, Ms. Hu Suzhen, Mrs. Zhu Shiming, Ms. Sun Wangguoxiu, Mrs. Huang Xiufeng, Ms. Yu Qingtang, Dr. Ni Weicong, Ms. Lu Shenyi, Mrs. Jin Longzhang, Mrs. Zhang Fuliang, Dr. Ge Chenghui, Ms. Yao Xianhui, Mrs. Zheng Zhangcheng, and Ms. Ding Shujing. Ms. Sun Wangguoxiu was publicly elected as the chairperson of the committee, and Ms. Hua Jingxia and Ms. You Cuibao were assigned as executive secretaries. A year passes quickly; thinking of the grand occasion at that time, it will surely be memorable.

St. John's to Hold Charity Dance 131

▲ Proceeds Donated to Northeast Volunteer Army

St. John's University in Van Royal Ferry will hold a Hawaiian Charity Dance at 8 p.m. on Saturday, November 19, in the school's Recreation Room. In addition to dancing, there will be special programs such as Hawaiian music, dancing by Sacred Heart Girls' School and Ms. Letterly, violin solo by Ms. Xia Luming, piano solo by Ms. Li Xianmin, solo singing by Miss Pierce, and hula dancing by St. John's students. Preliminary Hearing of Notorious Robber Ding Fubao and Others 132

▲ Mrs. Ding Liu Pays 3,000 Yuan Bail

▲ Lu Maoda and Six Others Released

Zhao Fuhai, a Chinese detective of the Xinzha Patrol Station, De Rong, and Bao Taiqian, a Western detective, successively arrested 18 men and women, including bandits Wang Zisheng and Wang Liutao, at No. 2 Tianxi Lane in Zhengjia Muqiao and the Zhongnan Hotel. They also seized four handguns and 29 bullets from the home of Ding Fubao at No. 3 Huacheng Lane on Min Ti Ni Yin Road. Subsequently, the First Special District Court, after releasing six people who were found to be unrelated, remanded the remaining 12 people in custody for further investigation. The details have been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, the date for the preliminary hearing arrived. The patrol station's lawyer, Wang Yaotang, presented the circumstances of the investigation, stating that the patrol station's investigation procedures for the defendants Wang Liutao and Zhang Kunjin were not yet complete, so he requested another extension. Wang Yusheng and Wang Wenxiang are now being prosecuted for gang robbery, because they allegedly organized a gang armed with weapons on September 26 of this year to rob the Puyi Rice Shop at No. 646 Kunming Road of 163 silver dollars, and on October 8, they were involved in an attempted armed robbery of a tailor shop at No. 614 Fuchang Lane on Yunnan Road. Ding Fubao and his wife, Ding Liu, are being prosecuted for violating gun control laws because handguns and bullets were found in their residence. However, the place where the guns and bullets were stored was equipped with a mechanism under the floor inside the door, with no traces, making it difficult to detect. Therefore, if Ding Fubao had not provided the information, the patrol station might not have discovered them yet. The remaining six people, including Lu Maoda and Zhou Tang, are also unrelated to the cases and requested to be released. The defendants, Jiang Yiping, Fan Gang, Tao Wuzhi, and other lawyers, appeared in court to defend them. Then, Lin Xianglin, the owner of Puyi Rice Shop, and Wang Wu Li, a domestic servant from the Yunnan Road Tailor Shop, filed reports, proving the circumstances of the robbery. When questioned, the two defendants, Wang Zisheng and Wang Wenxiang, confessed that the two robberies were initiated by Xue Sheng and Monk, who are at large, who took them to commit the robberies. The handguns were held by Xue Sheng and others, and they did not enter the premises. Afterwards, Xue Sheng gave them each 50 yuan, and so on. When questioned, Ding Fubao confessed that the seized guns and bullets were deposited at his place by Wang Zisheng. Ding Liu claimed to know nothing about the guns and bullets. Her agent, lawyer Jiang Yiping, requested that she be allowed to post bail first. Judge Ge Shixun verified the confessions and ordered that the case be adjourned for seven days for further hearing. Ding Liu was allowed to post 3,000 yuan bail for release. Lu Maoda and others were allowed to be released. Wang Zisheng, Wang Wenxiang, Ding Fubao, Wang Liutao, and Zhang Kunjin were remanded in custody at the patrol station.

Thirteen Robbers Apprehended in the Donghai Hotel 133

Lu Liankui, the Chinese Chief Inspector of the General Inspectorate of the General Patrol Station, learned that a large gang of kidnappers and bandits were hiding in the Donghai Hotel on Guangdong Road. He led Chinese detectives Liu Shaokui, Tang Jian, and others to the hotel secretly on the previous day. In Rooms 61, 64, and 68, they arrested 13 people, including Zhang Jiepu from Tongzhou, Gu Genlian, Zhang Amao, Tang Abao, Zhao Axiang, Song Mengsheng, Chen Heshang from Shanghai, Zhuang Ermu and Dai Xiaodi from Nanxiang, Yao Lianfu from Dachang, Lu Adong from Pudong, Wang Youtang from Changzhou, and Qiu Xiuying, a woman from Shanghai. They seized a handgun and five bullets and brought them back to the patrol station for separate detention. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Criminal Court of the First Special District. Presiding Judge Feng Shide and Chief Prosecutor Wang Zuze ascended the bench for the hearing. The patrol station's lawyer, Ru Baoyi, stated that he was requesting that all defendants in the case be detained, because the patrol station was short on time and had not yet begun investigating the crimes they committed. Once the investigation is complete, he will formally prosecute them in court. Judge Feng verified the report and briefly questioned each suspect, then ordered them to be detained and adjourned the hearing for another day.
